< Review>
Okay, I don't give many bad reviews, but this place deserves it today anyways. First I am greeted by female server. She asked me if I want to dine in or take out. I said dine in. She told me to wait. This is my first time here so I'm curious in what they have. I go ahead and help myself to the menu. The menu is uniquely formatted so I had alot of questions. The nice lady takes me to my seat, but then get distracted by other customers. I stand there in the middle the room for few minutes and then she starts an order for a large party. Dumbfounded, I took a seat at the bar where I was greeted by a male server and he said I'll help you in a minute. I wait and then he asks what I would like. I asked him about the customer favorites and what they were. He described the dishes for me and i decided to get the one that was "mostly meat" $2-7 more than the other ramen, but It should be worth it it's mostly meat. I was done ordering. He then goes back to the task he was doing before. I then look at the menu again and saw that there was add-ons. I was never told if I wanted any add-ons, but I looked at the menu and I guess I should have known. I wanted to ask about the add ons .  I was told to wait as he was having technical difficulties cool I understand. He finishes and  helps me out. I order my add ons and a side of curry rice. I then ask for some water. He says okay. Then starts filling up a  pitcher for another table, cool he'll get me in a sec. A few minutes pass by after serving that pitcher and no water. I then asked the Female server 3-4 times she said okay and the water never came. A bit irritated now. I find a solution and use sign language. I finally get my water. My food took about 20-30 mins to make but that doesn't matter to me as long as it's good. My food comes out and it's take out not dine in like I wanted. Slightly irritated, I take the L. As long as the food is good I say! First I'm looking at everything I got for $20. I'm feeling very disappointed. The regular rice is $1.50 for a cup. The curry rice is $4.50 you get a cup of rice and curry poored on top it wasn't worth the extra $3. I now start praying that the ramen can save me from this cruel world. The first thing I notice is its mostly veggies and only 2-3 slice's of meat! I did enjoy the meat, but for $2-7 more not worth it. The veggies were nothing special. I didn't get the wholesome, hearty taste you would get from fresh veggies. The broth of the Ramen wasn't my cup of tea. It had one flavor that I didn't enjoy personally. From my experience a good ramen has many flavors and smells. The noodles are good but not the best quality which Is made from scratch.< /Review>

Called the store and spoke to a VERY Rude guy and found out there are no spare links. I will have to buy them if I want to size it. Was extremely rude on the phone, said that is your problem and hanged up the phone. They only accept Wire transfers and checks, no credit cards. Should have known this was shady right there and then. The only reason I left 2 stars instead of one, is thank God I went to a local Rolex, bought the links and asked to check if they are real. They are, so that is good. Otherwise, my advise is stay away!!  Don't ever buy anything on line by check or wire unless you understand that you are on your own,. Check the BBB Reviews first!!! No complaints, no refunds, no nothing, just goodby, you are out of your money and the conversation is over. I buy designer watches every year but I will not buy from this place ever again!!!
